<!-- ✅ Autocomplete Scripts -->
<script src="https://code.jquery.com/ui/1.12.1/jquery-ui.js"></script>
<script>
$(function () {
  // === Treatment (Find Cost) ===
  $("#skill_input").autocomplete({
    source: "https://satyughealthcare.com/treatment_package/searchtreatment",
    select: function (event, ui) { $("#skill_input_value").val(ui.item.id); },
    change: function (event, ui) {
      $("#skill_input_value").val(ui.item.id);
      $("#skill_input").val(ui.item.value);
    }
  });

  // === Doctor Search ===
  $("#doctor").autocomplete({
    source: "https://satyughealthcare.com/doctor/search_doctor_list",
    select: function (event, ui) { $("#doctor_id_value").val(ui.item.id); },
    change: function (event, ui) {
      $("#doctor_id_value").val(ui.item.id);
      $("#doctor").val(ui.item.value);
    }
  });

  // ✅ FIXED: Autocomplete only on INPUT fields (not on <select> of hotel form)
  $("input#hospital, input#searchhospital").autocomplete({
    source: "https://satyughealthcare.com/hospital/search_hospital_list",
    select: function (event, ui) {
      if ($(this).attr('id') === 'hospital') {
        $("#hospital_value").val(ui.item.id);
      } else {
        $("#search_hospital_value").val(ui.item.id);
      }
    },
    change: function (event, ui) {
      if ($(this).attr('id') === 'hospital') {
        $("#hospital_value").val(ui.item.id);
        $("#hospital").val(ui.item.value);
      } else {
        $("#search_hospital_value").val(ui.item.id);
        $("#searchhospital").val(ui.item.value);
      }
    }
  });

  // === Treatment Search (Find Doctor) ===
  $("#treatment").autocomplete({
    source: "https://satyughealthcare.com/welcome/search_treatment_listing",
    select: function (event, ui) { $("#treatment_id_value").val(ui.item.id); },
    change: function (event, ui) {
      $("#treatment_id_value").val(ui.item.id);
      $("#treatment").val(ui.item.value);
    }
  });

  // === City (if used later) ===
  $("#city").autocomplete({
    source: "https://satyughealthcare.com/welcome/search_city_list",
    select: function (event, ui) { $("#city_value").val(ui.item.id); },
    change: function (event, ui) {
      $("#city_value").val(ui.item.id);
      $("#city").val(ui.item.value);
    }
  });
});
</script>

<script>
    // Lazy load videos on thumbnail click
    document.querySelectorAll('.video-thumbnail').forEach(thumbnail => {
        thumbnail.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const videoContainer = this.parentElement;
            const videoId = videoContainer.getAttribute('data-youtube');
            const iframe = `<iframe width="100%" height="315" 
                             src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/${videoId}?autoplay=1" 
                             frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" 
                             allowfullscreen></iframe>`;
            videoContainer.innerHTML = iframe; // Replace thumbnail with the video
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
         $("#insurance_page_url").val(window.location.href);
        $('#insurance_enquiry').submit(function() {
            $("#submit_insurance_enquiry").val("Loading...").prop('disabled', true);;
            $("#msg_insurance_enquiry").html();
            $.ajax({
                url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/insurance/enquiry",
                type: "POST",
                data: new FormData(this), // Data sent to server, a set of key/value pairs (i.e. form fields and values)
                contentType: false, // The content type used when sending data to the server.
                cache: false, // To unable request pages to be cached
                processData: false, // To send DOMDocument or non processed data file it is set to false
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function(response) { //console.log(response);
                     if(response['error']=='1'){
                        $('#msg_insurance_enquiry').html(response['msg']);
                        $("#submit_insurance_enquiry").val("Submit").prop('disabled', false);;
                     }else{
                        $('#msg_insurance_enquiry').html(response['msg']);
                        $('.reset_form').val('');
                        $("#submit_insurance_enquiry").prop('disabled', false).val("Submitted");
                        setTimeout(function() {
                           
                            $('#msg_insurance_enquiry').html();
                        }, 1000); 
                        setTimeout(function() {
                             $('#insurance_modal').modal('hide');
                        }, 3000);
                     }
                     
                    
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document.body).on('change',".file_upload",function (e) {
    	  $('.files').text('Uploaded');
    	
     });
         
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $("#page_url").val(window.location.href);
        $('#appointment_form').submit(function() {
            $("#appointment_form_submit").val("Loading...").prop('disabled', true);;
            $("#appointment_form_msg").html('');
            $.ajax({
                url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/Welcome/apointment_process",
                type: "POST",
                data: new FormData(this), // Data sent to server, a set of key/value pairs (i.e. form fields and values)
                contentType: false, // The content type used when sending data to the server.
                cache: false, // To unable request pages to be cached
                processData: false, // To send DOMDocument or non processed data file it is set to false
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function(response) { //console.log(response);
                     if(response['error']=='1'){
                        $('#appointment_form_msg').html(response['msg']);
                        $('#page_url').val(window.location.href); 
                        $("#appointment_form_submit").val("Submit").prop('disabled', false);;
                     }else{
                        $('#appointment_form_msg').html(response['msg']);
                        $('.reset_form').val('');
                         $('#page_url').val(window.location.href); 
                        $("#appointment_form_submit").prop('disabled', false).val("Submitted");
                        setTimeout(function() {
                           
                            $('#appointment_form_msg').html();
                        }, 1000); 
                        setTimeout(function() {
                             $('#Apointment').modal('hide');
                        }, 3000);
                     }
                     
                    
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    });
</script>

       $(document.body).on('click',".opinion_button",function (e) {
             var a = $(this) ; 
             var doctor_id = $(this).attr('data-id');
             $('#doctor_id').val(doctor_id).attr("selected", "selected")
      });

<script>
$(document).ready(function() {

    // Set page_url when modal opens
    $('#CallNowModel').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
        var currentUrl = window.location.href;   
        $(this).find('.page_url').val(currentUrl);
    });

    // Handle form submission
    $('#callNowForm').on('submit', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        $('#callNowFormmsg').html('');
        $("#callNowFormsubmit").text("Loading...").prop('disabled', true);

        $.ajax({
            url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/Welcome/enquiry",
            type: "POST",
            data: $(this).serialize(),
            success: function(response) {
                $("#callNowFormsubmit").text("SEND MESSAGE").prop('disabled', false);
                $('#callNowFormmsg').html(response);
                $('.reset_form').val('');
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $('#CallNowModel').modal('hide');
                }, 3000);
            },
            error: function() {
                $("#callNowFormsubmit").text("SEND MESSAGE").prop('disabled', false);
                $('#callNowFormmsg').html("<div class='alert alert-danger'>Something went wrong. Try again!</div>");
            }
        });
    });

});
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('#enquiry_for2').submit(function() {
            $("#submit2").val("Loading...");
            $.ajax({
                url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/contact/mail",
                type: "POST",
                data: new FormData(this), // Data sent to server, a set of key/value pairs (i.e. form fields and values)
                contentType: false, // The content type used when sending data to the server.
                cache: false, // To unable request pages to be cached
                processData: false, // To send DOMDocument or non processed data file it is set to false
                success: function(response) { //console.log(response);
                    $('#msg2').html(response);
                    $('.reset_form').val('');
                    $("#submit2").val("Submitted");

                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('#Apointment2').modal('hide')
                    }, 1500);
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    });
</script>
<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $(".phone").keydown(function(e) {
            // Allow: backspace, delete, tab, escape, enter and .
            if ($.inArray(e.keyCode, [46, 8, 9, 27, 13, 110]) !== -1 ||
                // Allow: Ctrl+A, Command+A
                (e.keyCode === 65 && (e.ctrlKey === true || e.metaKey === true)) ||
                // Allow: home, end, left, right, down, up
                (e.keyCode >= 35 && e.keyCode <= 40)) {
                // let it happen, don't do anything
                return;
            }
            // Ensure that it is a number and stop the keypress
            if ((e.shiftKey || (e.keyCode < 48 || e.keyCode > 57)) && (e.keyCode < 96 || e.keyCode > 105)) {
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

            },
            change: function(event, ui) {

            }
        });
    });

<script type="text/javascript">
      $('#state').on('change', function() {
        var stateID = $(this).val();
        if (stateID) {
          $.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: 'https://satyughealthcare.com/welcome/Get_city_OF_state',
            data: 'state_id=' + stateID,
            success: function(html) {
              $('#citylist').html(html);
            }
          });
        } else {
          $('#citylist').html('<option value="">Select state first</option>');
        }
      });
</script>

</html>        <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () { 
                $(document).on('click', '.show_more', function () {
                    $('.show_more').hide();
                    $('.loding').show();
                    var gender = get_filter('gender');
                    var relevance = get_filter('relevance');
                    var hospital_refid = get_filter('hospital_refid');
                    var treatment_refid = get_filter('treatment_refid');
                    var exp_year = get_filter('exp_year');
                    var city_id = get_filter('city_id');
                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: 'https://satyughealthcare.com/doctor/loadmore',
                        data: {
                            relevance: relevance,
                            hospital_refid: hospital_refid,
                            treatment_refid: treatment_refid,
                            exp_year: exp_year,
                            gender: gender,
                            city_id: city_id,
                            id: ID
                        },
                        success: function (html) {
                            $('#show_more_main' + ID)
                                .remove();
                            $('.postList')
                                .append(html);
                        }
                    });
                });
                $(document).on('click', '#clearall,#clearall2,#clearall3', function () {
                    var relevance = '';
                    var hospital_refid = '';
                    var treatment_refid = '';
                    var exp_year = '';
                    var gender = '';
                    var city_id = '';
                    var page_num = 0;
                    $.ajax({
                        url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/doctor/ajaxPaginationData/",
                        data: {
                            relevance: relevance,
                            hospital_refid: hospital_refid,
                            treatment_refid: treatment_refid,
                            exp_year: exp_year,
                            gender: gender,
                            city_id: city_id,
                            page: page_num,
                        },
                        beforeSend: function(){
                            $('.loading').show();
                        },
                        success: function (data) {
                            $('.postList') .html(data);
                            $('.loading').fadeOut("slow");
                            clearSelected('relevance');
                            clearSelected('hospital_refid');
                            clearSelected('treatment_refid');
                            clearSelected('exp_year');
                            clearSelected('gender');
                            clearSelected('city_id');    
                        }
                      
                    });
                });

                function clearSelected($a) {
                    $('.' + $a).find($('option')).attr('selected', false)
                }

                
            });


            function searchFilter(page_num){
                       page_num = page_num?page_num:0;

                        var gender = get_filter('gender');
                        var relevance = get_filter('relevance');
                        var hospital_refid = get_filter('hospital_refid');
                        var treatment_refid = get_filter('treatment_refid');
                        var exp_year = get_filter('exp_year');
                        var city_id = get_filter('city_id');
                        $.ajax({
                            url: "https://satyughealthcare.com/doctor/ajaxPaginationData/"+page_num,
                            method: "POST",
                            data: {
                                relevance: relevance,
                                hospital_refid: hospital_refid,
                                treatment_refid: treatment_refid,
                                exp_year: exp_year,
                                gender: gender,
                                city_id: city_id,
                                page: page_num,
                            },
                             beforeSend: function(){
                                $('.loading').show();
                            },
                            success: function (data) {
                                $('.postList') .html(data);
                                $('.loading').fadeOut("slow");    
                            }
                        });
            }

        

            function get_filter(class_name) {
                var filter = [];
                filter = $('.' + class_name).val();
                return filter;
            }

        </script>
